style="height: 0.336108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord text mtight"><span class="mord mtight">left&nbsp;</span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">⇒</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mord">0</span><span class="mclose delimcenter" style="top: 0em;">]</span></span></span></span><span class="" style="top: -4.29145em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3.50429em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mord">1</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span><span class="mbin">−</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span><span class="mop"><span class="mord mathrm">P</span><span class="mord mathrm">r</span></span><span class="mopen">[</span><span class="mord text"><span class="mord">&nbsp;all&nbsp;</span></span><span class="mord mathdefault" style="margin-right: 0.03588em;">q</span><span class="mord text"><span class="mord">&nbsp;independent&nbsp;calls&nbsp;to&nbsp;PREDICT&nbsp;return&nbsp;</span></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathrm" style="margin-right: 0.07778em;">f</span><span class="mord mathrm">a</span><span class="mord mathrm">l</span><span class="mord mathrm">s</span><span class="mord mathrm">e</span></span><span class="mclose">]</span></span></span><span class="" style="top: -2.12716em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3.50429em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mord">1</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span><span class="mbin">−</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span><span class="minner"><span class="minner"><span class="mopen delimcenter" style="top: 0em;"><span class="delimsizing size3">(</span></span><span class="mord">1</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span><span class="mbin">−</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mopen nulldelimiter"></span><span class="mfrac"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 1.32144em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.314em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord">2</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.775108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.989em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathdefault mtight">λ</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="" style="top: -3.23em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="frac-line" style="border-bottom-width: 0.04em;"></span></span><span class="" style="top: -3.677em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord">1</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.686em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mclose nulldelimiter"></span></span><span class="mclose delimcenter" style="top: 0em;"><span class="delimsizing size3">)</span></span></span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 1.50429em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.9029em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathdefault mtight" style="margin-right: 0.03588em;">q</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 2.62716em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><br>
Rather than understand this probability, we can just compute an upper bound for it. Using the union bound, we get:<br>
<span class="katex--display"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mtable rowspacing="0.24999999999999992em" columnalign="right left" columnspacing="0em"><mtr><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="true"><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">Pr</mi><mo>⁡</mo><mrow><mo fence="true">[</mo><msub><mi mathvariant="script">A</mi><mtext>obvious&nbsp;</mtext></msub><mo>⋄</mo><msub><mi mathvariant="script">L</mi><mtext>left&nbsp;</mtext></msub><mo>⇒</mo><mn>1</mn><mo fence="true">]</mo></mrow></mrow></mstyle></mtd><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="true"><mrow><mrow></mrow><mo>⩽</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">Pr</mi><mo>⁡</mo><mo stretchy="false">[</mo><mtext>&nbsp;first&nbsp;call&nbsp;to&nbsp;PREDICT&nbsp;returns&nbsp;true&nbsp;</mtext><mo stretchy="false">]</mo></mrow></mstyle></mtd></mtr><mtr><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="true"><mrow></mrow></mstyle></mtd><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="true"><mrow><mrow></mrow><mo>+</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">Pr</mi><mo>⁡</mo><mo stretchy="false">[</mo><mtext>&nbsp;second&nbsp;call&nbsp;to&nbsp;PREDICT&nbsp;returns&nbsp;true&nbsp;</mtext><mo stretchy="false">]</mo><mo>+</mo><mo>⋯</mo></mrow></mstyle></mtd></mtr><mtr><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="true"><mrow></mrow></mstyle></mtd><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="true"><mrow><mrow></mrow><mo>=</mo><mi>q</mi><mfrac><mn>1</mn><msup><mn>2</mn><mi>λ</mi></msup></mfrac></mrow></mstyle></mtd></mtr></mtable><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">
\begin{aligned}
\operatorname{Pr}\left[\mathcal{A}_{\text {obvious }} \diamond \mathcal{L}_{\text {left }} \Rightarrow 1\right]&amp; \leqslant \operatorname{Pr}[\text { first call to PREDICT returns true }] \\
&amp;+\operatorname{Pr}[\text { second call to PREDICT returns true }]+\cdots \\
&amp;=q \frac{1}{2^{\lambda}}
\end{aligned}
</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 5.30744em; vertical-align: -2.40372em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mtable"><span class="col-align-r"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 2.90372em;"><span class="" style="top: -5.38516em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3.32144em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mop"><span class="mord mathrm">P</span><span class="mord mathrm">r</span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.166667em;"></span><span class="minner"><span class="mopen delimcenter" style="top: 0em;">[</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathcal">A</span></span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.336108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord text mtight"><span class="mord mtight">obvious&nbsp;</span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span><span class="mbin">⋄</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathcal">L</span></span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.336108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord text mtight"><span class="mord mtight">left&nbsp;</span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">⇒</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mord">1</span><span class="mclose delimcenter" style="top: 0em;">]</span></span></span></span><span class="" style="top: -3.88516em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3.32144em;"></span><span class="mord"></span></span><span class="" style="top: -1.90372em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3.32144em;"></span><span class="mord"></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 2.40372em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span><span class="col-align-l"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 2.90372em;"><span class="" style="top: -5.38516em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3.32144em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel amsrm">⩽</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mop"><span class="mord mathrm">P</span><span class="mord mathrm">r</span></span><span class="mopen">[</span><span class="mord text"><span class="mord">&nbsp;first&nbsp;call&nbsp;to&nbsp;PREDICT&nbsp;returns&nbsp;true&nbsp;</span></span><span class="mclose">]</span></span></span><span class="" style="top: -3.88516em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3.32144em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span><span class="mbin">+</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span><span class="mop"><span class="mord mathrm">P</span><span class="mord mathrm">r</span></span><span class="mopen">[</span><span class="mord text"><span class="mord">&nbsp;second&nbsp;call&nbsp;to&nbsp;PREDICT&nbsp;returns&nbsp;true&nbsp;</span></span><span class="mclose">]</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span><span class="mbin">+</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span><span class="minner">⋯</span></span></span><span class="" style="top: -1.90372em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3.32144em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault" style="margin-right: 0.03588em;">q</span><span class="mord"><span class="mopen nulldelimiter"></span><span class="mfrac"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 1.32144em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.314em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord">2</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.775108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.989em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathdefault mtight">λ</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="" style="top: -3.23em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="frac-line" style="border-bottom-width: 0.04em;"></span></span><span class="" style="top: -3.677em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord">1</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.686em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mclose nulldelimiter"></span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 2.40372em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><br>
This is an overestimate of some probabilities (e.g., if the rst call to predict returns true, then the second call isn’t made). More fundamentally, <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>q</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">/</mi><msup><mn>2</mn><mi>λ</mi></msup></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">q/2^\lambda</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1.09911em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault" style="margin-right: 0.03588em;">q</span><span class="mord">/</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord">2</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.849108em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.063em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathdefault mtight">λ</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span>  exceeds 1 when <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>q</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">q</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.625em; vertical-align: -0.19444em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault" style="margin-right: 0.03588em;">q</span></span></span></span></span> is large. But nevertheless, <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mtext>Pr</mtext><mo stretchy="false">[</mo><msub><mi mathvariant="script">A</mi><mtext>obvious</mtext></msub><mo>⋄</mo><msub><mi mathvariant="script">L</mi><mtext>left</mtext></msub><mo>⇒</mo><mn>1</mn><mo stretchy="false">]</mo><mo>⩽</mo><mi>q</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">/</mi><msup><mn>2</mn><mi>λ</mi></msup><mi mathvariant="normal">.</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\text{Pr}[\mathcal{A}_{\text{obvious}}\diamond \mathcal{L}_{\text{left}}\Rightarrow 1]\leqslant q/2^\lambda.</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mord text"><span class="mord">Pr</span></span><span class="mopen">[</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathcal">A</span></span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.336108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord text mtight"><span class="mord mtight">obvious</span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span><span class="mbin">⋄</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.83333em; vertical-align: -0.15em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathcal">L</span></span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.336108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord text mtight"><span class="mord mtight">left</span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">⇒</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mord">1</span><span class="mclose">]</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel amsrm">⩽</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1.09911em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault" style="margin-right: 0.03588em;">q</span><span class="mord">/</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord">2</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.849108em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.063em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathdefault mtight">λ</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mord">.</span></span></span></span></span></li>
</ul>
<p><em>We showed that <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><msub><mi mathvariant="script">A</mi><mtext>obvious</mtext></msub></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathcal{A}_{\text{obvious}}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.83333em; vertical-align: -0.15em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathcal">A</span></span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.336108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord text mtight"><span class="mord mtight">obvious</span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span> has non-zero advantage. This is enough to show that <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><msub><mi mathvariant="script">L</mi><mtext>left</mtext></msub><mi mathvariant="normal">≠</mi><msub><mi mathvariant="script">L</mi><mtext>right</mtext></msub></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathcal{L}_{\text{left}}\neq\mathcal{L}_{\text{right}}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.88888em; vertical-align: -0.19444em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathcal">L</span></span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.336108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord text mtight"><span class="mord mtight">left</span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel"><span class="mrel"><span class="mord"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.69444em;"><span class="" style="top: -3em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="rlap"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.88888em; vertical-align: -0.19444em;"></span><span class="inner"><span class="mrel"></span></span><span class="fix"></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.19444em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mrel">=</span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.969438em; vertical-align: -0.286108em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathcal">L</span></span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.336108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord text mtight"><span class="mord mtight">right</span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.286108em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span>.<br>
We also showed that <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><msub><mi mathvariant="script">A</mi><mtext>obvious</mtext></msub></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathcal{A}_{\text{obvious}}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.83333em; vertical-align: -0.15em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathcal">A</span></span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.336108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord text mtight"><span class="mord mtight">obvious</span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span> has advantage at most <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>q</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">/</mi><msup><mn>2</mn><mi>λ</mi></msup></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">q/2^\lambda</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1.09911em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault" style="margin-right: 0.03588em;">q</span><span class="mord">/</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord">2</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.849108em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.063em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathdefault mtight">λ</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span>. Since <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><msub><mi mathvariant="script">A</mi><mtext>obvious</mtext></msub></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathcal{A}_{\text{obvious}}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.83333em; vertical-align: -0.15em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathcal">A</span></span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.336108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord text mtight"><span class="mord mtight">obvious</span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span> runs in polynomial<br>
time, it can only make a polynomial number q of queries to the library, so <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>q</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">/</mi><msup><mn>2</mn><mi>λ</mi></msup></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">q/2^\lambda</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1.09911em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault" style="margin-right: 0.03588em;">q</span><span class="mord">/</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord">2</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.849108em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.063em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathdefault mtight">λ</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span> is negligible. However, this is not enough to show that <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><msub><mi mathvariant="script">L</mi><mtext>left</mtext></msub><mo>≈</mo><msub><mi mathvariant="script">L</mi><mtext>right</mtext></msub></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathcal{L}_{\text{left}}\approx\mathcal{L}_{\text{right}}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.83333em; vertical-align: -0.15em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathcal">L</span></span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.336108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord text mtight"><span class="mord mtight">left</span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">≈</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.969438em; vertical-align: -0.286108em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathcal">L</span></span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.336108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord text mtight"><span class="mord mtight">right</span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.286108em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span> since it considers only <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>a</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">a</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.43056em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault">a</span></span></span></span></span> single calling program. To show that the libraries are indistinguishable, we must show that <strong>every</strong> calling program’s advantage is negligible.</em></p>
<p>In a few pages, we will prove that for any <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi mathvariant="script">A</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathcal{A}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.68333em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathcal">A</span></span></span></span></span></span> that makes <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>q</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">q</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.625em; vertical-align: -0.19444em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault" style="margin-right: 0.03588em;">q</span></span></span></span></span> calls to PREDICT,<br>
<span class="katex--display"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mrow><mo fence="true">∣</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">Pr</mi><mo>⁡</mo><mrow><mo fence="true">[</mo><mi mathvariant="script">F</mi><mo>⋄</mo><msub><mi mathvariant="script">L</mi><mtext>left&nbsp;</mtext></msub><mo>⇒</mo><mn>1</mn><mo fence="true">]</mo></mrow><mo>−</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">Pr</mi><mo>⁡</mo><mrow><mo fence="true">[</mo><mi mathvariant="script">A</mi><mo>⋄</mo><msub><mi mathvariant="script">L</mi><mtext>right&nbsp;</mtext></msub><mo>⇒</mo><mn>1</mn><mo fence="true">]</mo></mrow><mo fence="true">∣</mo></mrow><mo>⩽</mo><mfrac><mi>q</mi><msup><mn>2</mn><mi>λ</mi></msup></mfrac><mi mathvariant="normal">.</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">
\left|\operatorname{Pr}\left[\mathcal{F} \diamond \mathcal{L}_{\text {left }} \Rightarrow 1\right]-\operatorname{Pr}\left[\mathcal{A} \diamond \mathcal{L}_{\text {right }} \Rightarrow 1\right]\right| \leqslant \frac{q}{2^{\lambda}}.
</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1.03611em; vertical-align: -0.286108em;"></span><span class="minner"><span class="mopen delimcenter" style="top: 0em;">∣</span><span class="mop"><span class="mord mathrm">P</span><span class="mord mathrm">r</span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.166667em;"></span><span class="minner"><span class="mopen delimcenter" style="top: 0em;">[</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathcal" style="margin-right: 0.09931em;">F</span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span><span class="mbin">⋄</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathcal">L</span></span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.336108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord text mtight"><span class="mord mtight">left&nbsp;</span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">⇒</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mord">1</span><span class="mclose delimcenter" style="top: 0em;">]</span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span><span class="mbin">−</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span><span class="mop"><span class="mord mathrm">P</span><span class="mord mathrm">r</span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.166667em;"></span><span class="minner"><span class="mopen delimcenter" style="top: 0em;">[</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathcal">A</span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span><span class="mbin">⋄</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathcal">L</span></span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.336108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord text mtight"><span class="mord mtight">right&nbsp;</span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.286108em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">⇒</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mord">1</span><span class="mclose delimcenter" style="top: 0em;">]</span></span><span class="mclose delimcenter" style="top: 0em;">∣</span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel amsrm">⩽</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1.79356em; vertical-align: -0.686em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mopen nulldelimiter"></span><span class="mfrac"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 1.10756em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.314em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord">2</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.775108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.989em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathdefault mtight">λ</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="" style="top: -3.23em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="frac-line" style="border-bottom-width: 0.04em;"></span></span><span class="" style="top: -3.677em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathdefault" style="margin-right: 0.03588em;">q</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.686em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mclose nulldelimiter"></span></span><span class="mord">.</span></span></span></span></span></span><br>
For any polynomial-time <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi mathvariant="script">A</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathcal{A}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.68333em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathcal">A</span></span></span></span></span></span>, the number <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>q</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">q</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.625em; vertical-align: -0.19444em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault" style="margin-right: 0.03588em;">q</span></span></span></span></span> of calls to PREDICT will be a polynomial in <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>λ</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\lambda</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.69444em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault">λ</span></span></span></span></span>, making <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>q</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">/</mi><msup><mn>2</mn><mi>λ</mi></msup></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">q/2^\lambda</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1.09911em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault" style="margin-right: 0.03588em;">q</span><span class="mord">/</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord">2</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.849108em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.063em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathdefault mtight">λ</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span> a negligible function. Hence, <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><msub><mi mathvariant="script">L</mi><mtext>left</mtext></msub><mo>≈</mo><msub><mi mathvariant="script">L</mi><mtext>right</mtext></msub></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathcal{L}_{\text{left}}\approx\mathcal{L}_{\text{right}}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.83333em; vertical-align: -0.15em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathcal">L</span></span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.336108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord text mtight"><span class="mord mtight">left</span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">≈</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.969438em; vertical-align: -0.286108em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathcal">L</span></span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.336108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord text mtight"><span class="mord mtight">right</span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.286108em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span>.</p>
<h3 id="other-properties">Other Properties</h3>
<p><strong>Lemma 4.6(<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mo>≈</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\bf{\approx}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.48312em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mrel">≈</span></span></span></span></span></span></span> facts)</strong><br>
<span class="katex--display"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mtext>&nbsp;If&nbsp;</mtext><msub><mi mathvariant="script">L</mi><mn>1</mn></msub><mo>≡</mo><msub><mi mathvariant="script">L</mi><mn>2</mn></msub><mtext>&nbsp;then&nbsp;</mtext><msub><mi mathvariant="script">L</mi><mn>1</mn></msub><mo>≈</mo><msub><mi mathvariant="script">L</mi><mn>2</mn></msub><mi mathvariant="normal">.</mi><mtext>&nbsp;Also,&nbsp;if&nbsp;</mtext><msub><mi mathvariant="script">L</mi><mn>1</mn></msub><mo>≈</mo><msub><mi mathvariant="script">L</mi><mn>2</mn></msub><mo>≈</mo><msub><mi mathvariant="script">L</mi><mn>3</mn></msub><mtext>&nbsp;then&nbsp;</mtext><msub><mi mathvariant="script">L</mi><mn>1</mn></msub><mo>≈</mo><msub><mi mathvariant="script">L</mi><mn>3</mn></msub></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">
\text { If } \mathcal{L}_{1} \equiv \mathcal{L}_{2} \text { then } \mathcal{L}_{1} \approx \mathcal{L}_{2} . \text { Also, if } \mathcal{L}_{1} \approx \mathcal{L}_{2} \approx \mathcal{L}_{3} \text { then } \mathcal{L}_{1} \approx \mathcal{L}_{3}
</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.84444em; vertical-align: -0.15em;"></span><span class="mord text"><span class="mord">&nbsp;If&nbsp;</span></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathcal">L</span></span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.301108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mtight">1</span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">≡</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.84444em; vertical-align: -0.15em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathcal">L</span></span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.301108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mtight">2</span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mord text"><span class="mord">&nbsp;then&nbsp;</span></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathcal">L</span></span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.301108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mtight">1</span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">≈</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.88888em; vertical-align: -0.19444em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathcal">L</span></span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.301108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mtight">2</span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mord">.</span><span class="mord text"><span class="mord">&nbsp;Also,&nbsp;if&nbsp;</span></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathcal">L</span></span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.301108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mtight">1</span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">≈</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.83333em; vertical-align: -0.15em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathcal">L</span></span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.301108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mtight">2</span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">≈</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.84444em; vertical-align: -0.15em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathcal">L</span></span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.301108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mtight">3</span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mord text"><span class="mord">&nbsp;then&nbsp;</span></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathcal">L</span></span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.301108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mtight">1</span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">≈</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.83333em; vertical-align: -0.15em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathcal">L</span></span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.301108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mtight">3</span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><br>
Analogous to Lemma 2.11, we also have the following library chaining lemma, which you are asked to prove as an exercise:</p>
<p><strong>Lemma 4.7 (Chaining)</strong><br>
If <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><msub><mi mathvariant="script">L</mi><mtext>left</mtext></msub><mo>≈</mo><msub><mi mathvariant="script">L</mi><mtext>right</mtext></msub></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathcal{L}_{\text{left}}\approx\mathcal{L}_{\text{right}}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.83333em; vertical-align: -0.15em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathcal">L</span></span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.336108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord text mtight"><span class="mord mtight">left</span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">≈</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.969438em; vertical-align: -0.286108em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathcal">L</span></span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.336108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord text mtight"><span class="mord mtight">right</span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.286108em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span> then <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><msup><mi mathvariant="script">L</mi><mo>∗</mo></msup><mo>⋄</mo><msub><mi mathvariant="script">L</mi><mtext>left</mtext></msub><mo>≈</mo><msup><mi mathvariant="script">L</mi><mo>∗</mo></msup><mo>⋄</mo><msub><mi mathvariant="script">L</mi><mtext>right</mtext></msub></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathcal{L}^*\diamond \mathcal{L}_{\text{left}}\approx\mathcal{L}^*\diamond\mathcal{L}_{\text{right}}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.688696em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathcal">L</span></span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.688696em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.063em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mbin mtight">∗</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span><span class="mbin">⋄</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.83333em; vertical-align: -0.15em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathcal">L</span></span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.336108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord text mtight"><span class="mord mtight">left</span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">≈</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.688696em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathcal">L</span></span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.688696em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.063em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mbin mtight">∗</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span><span class="mbin">⋄</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.969438em; vertical-align: -0.286108em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathcal">L</span></span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.336108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord text mtight"><span class="mord mtight">right</span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.286108em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span> for any polynomial-time library <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><msup><mi mathvariant="script">L</mi><mo>∗</mo></msup></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathcal{L}^*</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.688696em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathcal">L</span></span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.688696em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.063em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mbin mtight">∗</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span>.</p>
<h3 id="bad-event-lemma">Bad-Event Lemma</h3>
<p>A common situation is when two libraries are expected to execute exactly the same statements, until some rare &amp; exceptional condition happens. In that case, we can bound an attacker’s distinguishing advantage by the probability of the exceptional condition.</p>
<p>More formally,</p>
<p><strong>Lemma 4.8 (Bad events)</strong><br>
<em>Let <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><msub><mi mathvariant="script">L</mi><mtext>left</mtext></msub></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathcal{L}_{\text{left}}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.83333em; vertical-align: -0.15em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathcal">L</span></span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.336108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord text mtight"><span class="mord mtight">left</span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span> and <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><msub><mi mathvariant="script">L</mi><mtext>right</mtext></msub></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathcal{L}_{\text{right}}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.969438em; vertical-align: -0.286108em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathcal">L</span></span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.336108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord text mtight"><span class="mord mtight">right</span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.286108em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span> be libraries that each dene a variable named ‘bad’ that is initialized to 0. If <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><msub><mi mathvariant="script">L</mi><mtext>left</mtext></msub></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathcal{L}_{\text{left}}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.83333em; vertical-align: -0.15em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathcal">L</span></span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.336108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord text mtight"><span class="mord mtight">left</span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span> and <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><msub><mi mathvariant="script">L</mi><mtext>right</mtext></msub></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathcal{L}_{\text{right}}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.969438em; vertical-align: -0.286108em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathcal">L</span></span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.336108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord text mtight"><span class="mord mtight">right</span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.286108em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span>  have identical code, except for code blocks reachable only when bad = 1 (e.g., guarded by an “if bad = 1” statement), then</em></p>
<p><span class="katex--display"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mrow><mo fence="true">∣</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">Pr</mi><mo>⁡</mo><mrow><mo fence="true">[</mo><mi mathvariant="script">A</mi><mo>⋄</mo><msub><mi mathvariant="script">L</mi><mtext>left&nbsp;</mtext></msub><mo>⇒</mo><mn>1</mn><mo fence="true">]</mo></mrow><mo>−</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">Pr</mi><mo>⁡</mo><mrow><mo fence="true">[</mo><mi mathvariant="script">A</mi><mo>⋄</mo><msub><mi mathvariant="script">L</mi><mtext>right&nbsp;</mtext></msub><mo>⇒</mo><mn>1</mn><mo fence="true">]</mo></mrow><mo fence="true">∣</mo></mrow><mo>⩽</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">Pr</mi><mo>⁡</mo><mrow><mo fence="true">[</mo><mi mathvariant="script">A</mi><mo>⋄</mo><msub><mi mathvariant="script">L</mi><mtext>left&nbsp;</mtext></msub><mtext>&nbsp;sets&nbsp;bad&nbsp;</mtext><mo>=</mo><mn>1</mn><mo fence="true">]</mo></mrow></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">
\left|\operatorname{Pr}\left[\mathcal{A} \diamond \mathcal{L}_{\text {left }} \Rightarrow 1\right]-\operatorname{Pr}\left[\mathcal{A} \diamond \mathcal{L}_{\text {right }} \Rightarrow 1\right]\right| \leqslant \operatorname{Pr}\left[\mathcal{A} \diamond \mathcal{L}_{\text {left }} \text { sets bad }=1\right]
</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1.03611em; vertical-align: -0.286108em;"></span><span class="minner"><span class="mopen delimcenter" style="top: 0em;">∣</span><span class="mop"><span class="mord mathrm">P</span><span class="mord mathrm">r</span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.166667em;"></span><span class="minner"><span class="mopen delimcenter" style="top: 0em;">[</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathcal">A</span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span><span class="mbin">⋄</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathcal">L</span></span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.336108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord text mtight"><span class="mord mtight">left&nbsp;</span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">⇒</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mord">1</span><span class="mclose delimcenter" style="top: 0em;">]</span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span><span class="mbin">−</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span><span class="mop"><span class="mord mathrm">P</span><span class="mord mathrm">r</span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.166667em;"></span><span class="minner"><span class="mopen delimcenter" style="top: 0em;">[</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathcal">A</span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span><span class="mbin">⋄</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathcal">L</span></span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.336108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord text mtight"><span class="mord mtight">right&nbsp;</span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.286108em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">⇒</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mord">1</span><span class="mclose delimcenter" style="top: 0em;">]</span></span><span class="mclose delimcenter" style="top: 0em;">∣</span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel amsrm">⩽</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mop"><span class="mord mathrm">P</span><span class="mord mathrm">r</span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.166667em;"></span><span class="minner"><span class="mopen delimcenter" style="top: 0em;">[</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathcal">A</span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span><span class="mbin">⋄</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathcal">L</span></span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.336108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord text mtight"><span class="mord mtight">left&nbsp;</span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mord text"><span class="mord">&nbsp;sets&nbsp;bad&nbsp;</span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mord">1</span><span class="mclose delimcenter" style="top: 0em;">]</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>
<p><strong><span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mo>⋆</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\bf{\star}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.46528em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord">⋆</span></span></span></span></span></span></span>Proof</strong><br>
Fix an arbitrary calling program <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi mathvariant="script">A</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathcal{A}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.68333em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathcal">A</span></span></span></span></span></span>. In this proof, we use conditional probabilites to isolate the cases where bad is changed to 1. We define the following events:</p>
<ul>
<li><span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><msub><mi mathvariant="script">B</mi><mtext>left</mtext></msub></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathcal{B}_{\text{left}}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.83333em; <p>We also write  <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mover accent="true"><msub><mi mathvariant="script">B</mi><mtext>left</mtext></msub><mo stretchy="true">‾</mo></mover></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\overline{\mathcal{B}_{\text{left}}}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1.03333em; vertical-align: -0.15em;"></span><span class="mord overline"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.88333em;"><span class="" style="top: -3em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathcal" style="margin-right: 0.03041em;">B</span></span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.336108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord text mtight"><span class="mord mtight">left</span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="" style="top: -3.80333em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="overline-line" style="border-bottom-width: 0.04em;"></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span> and <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mover accent="true"><msub><mi mathvariant="script">B</mi><mtext>right</mtext></msub><mo stretchy="true">‾</mo></mover></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\overline{\mathcal{B}_{\text{right}}}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1.16944em; vertical-align: -0.286108em;"></span><span class="mord overline"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.88333em;"><span class="" style="top: -3em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathcal" style="margin-right: 0.03041em;">B</span></span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.336108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; From conditional probability, we can write:<br>

mathvariant="script">L</mi><mtext>right&nbsp;</mtext></msub><mo>⇒</mo><mn>1</mn><mo>∣</mo><mover accent="true"><msub><mi mathvariant="script">B</mi><mtext>right&nbsp;</mtext></msub><mo stretchy="true">‾</mo></mover><mo fence="true">]</mo></mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">Pr</mi><mo>⁡</mo><mrow><mo fence="true">[</mo><mover accent="true"><msub><mi mathvariant="script">B</mi><mtext>right&nbsp;</mtext></msub><mo stretchy="true">‾</mo></mover><mo fence="true">]</mo></mrow></mrow></mstyle></mtd></mtr></mtable><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">
\begin{array}{lll}
\operatorname{Pr}\left[\mathcal{A} \diamond \mathcal{L}_{\text {left }} \Rightarrow 1\right]&amp;=&amp;\operatorname{Pr}\left[\mathcal{A} \diamond \mathcal{L}_{\text {left }} \Rightarrow 1 \mid \mathcal{B}_{\text {left }}\right] \operatorname{Pr}\left[\mathcal{B}_{\text {left }}\right] \\
&amp;&amp;+\operatorname{Pr}\left[\mathcal{A} \diamond \mathcal{L}_{\text {left }} \Rightarrow 1 \mid \overline{\mathcal{B}_{\text {left }}}\right] \operatorname{Pr}\left[\overline{\mathcal{B}_{\text {left }}}\right] \\
\operatorname{Pr}\left[\mathcal{A} \diamond \mathcal{L}_{\text {right }} \Rightarrow 1\right]&amp;=&amp;\operatorname{Pr}\left[\mathcal{A} \diamond \mathcal{L}_{\text {right }} \Rightarrow 1 \mid \mathcal{B}_{\text {right }}\right] \operatorname{Pr}\left[\mathcal{B}_{\text {right }}\right] \\
&amp;&amp;+\operatorname{Pr}\left[\mathcal{A} \diamond \mathcal{L}_{\text {right }} \Rightarrow 1 \mid \overline{\mathcal{B}_{\text {right }}}\right] \operatorname{Pr}\left[\overline{\mathcal{B}_{\text {right }}}\right]
\end{array}

style="top: -2.55em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord text
